#Keizo Obuchi suffers a stroke
country_event = {
	id = japan_classic.15
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event japan_classic.15" }
	title = japan_classic.15.t
	desc = japan_classic.15.d
	picture = GFX_hospital
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		has_country_leader = { name = "Keizo Obuchi" }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = japan_classic.16 days = 3 } }
	}
	
	option = {	#Let's pray for the best
		name = japan_classic.15.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: japan_classic.15.o1 executed"
		add_stability = -0.02
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = japan_classic.16
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event japan_classic.16" }
	title = japan_classic.16.t
	desc = japan_classic.16.d
	# TODO:picture change
	picture = GFX_yoshiro_mori
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = japan_classic.16.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: japan_classic.16.o1 executed"
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { 
					ruling_party = 0 
				} 
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yoshiro Mori" 
				picture = "yoshiro_mori.dds" 
				ideology = Western_Autocracy
				traits = {
					western_conservatism 
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { 
					ruling_party = 1 
				} 
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yoshiro Mori" 
				picture = "yoshiro_mori.dds" 
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism 
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { 
					ruling_party = 6 
				} 
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yoshiro Mori" 
				picture = "yoshiro_mori.dds" 
				ideology = Conservative
				traits = {
					western_conservatism 
				}
			}
		}
		
	}
}

#Yoshirō Mori's Emperor gaffe
country_event = {
	id = japan_classic.18
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event japan_classic.18" }
	title = japan_classic.18.t
	desc = japan_classic.18.d
	# TODO:picture change
	picture = GFX_yoshiro_mori
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_leader = { name = "Yoshiro Mori" }
	}
	
	option = {	#What a fool!
		name = japan_classic.18.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: japan_classic.18.o1 executed"
		add_stability = -0.01
		add_political_power = -10
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.03 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
	}
	
	option = {	#Double down on his statement
		name = japan_classic.18.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: japan_classic.18.o2 executed"
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = nationalist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_stability = -0.04
		add_political_power = -25
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
	}
}

#2000 Tottori Earthquake
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.121006001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.121006001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.121006001.d
	#TODO picture
	
	trigger = {
		controls_state = 611 
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		611 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 1.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	#National Aid
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.disaster_help
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.121006001 - disaster_help"
		add_to_variable = { debt = 1.0 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_add_debt_disaster1_TT
		ai_chance = {
			 base = 75 
		}
	}
	
	#Self-Determination
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.disaster_leave
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.121006001 - disaster_leave"
		add_stability = -0.01
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

#Ehime-Maru Disaster
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.130210001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.130210001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.130210001.d
	#TODO picture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#action
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.130210001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.130210001.oA"
		add_political_power = -10
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				has_country_leader = { name = "Yoshiro Mori" }	
				factor = 0
			}	
		}
	}
	
	#golf
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.130210001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.130210001.oB"
		add_stability = -0.03
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_leader = {
					 name = "Yoshiro Mori" 
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_PROGOLFER_MORI
			custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_koizumi_appear_TT
		}
	
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

#2001 Geiyo Earthquake
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.130324001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.130324001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.130324001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		controls_state = 611 
		controls_state = 610
	}
	
	immediate = {
		611 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 1.0
			}
			damage_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				damage = 0.5
			}
		}
		610 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 0.1
			}
		}
	}
	
	#National Aid
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.disaster_help
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.130324001 - disaster_help"
		add_to_variable = { debt = 1.0 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_add_debt_disaster1_TT
		ai_chance = { 
			base = 75
		 }
	}
	
	#Self-Determination
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.disaster_leave
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.130324001 - disaster_leave"
		add_stability = -0.01
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = JAP_historical.20010426
	title = JAP_historical.20010426.t
	desc = JAP_historical.20010426.d
	#TODO:picture 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_country_leader = { name = "Yoshiro Mori" }	
			has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_PROGOLFER_MORI
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = JAP_historical.20010426.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: JAP_historical.20010426.oA executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { 
					ruling_party = 0 
				} 
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Junichiro Koizumi"
				picture = "junichiro_koizumi.dds"
				ideology = Western_Autocracy
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { 
					ruling_party = 1 
				} 
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Junichiro Koizumi"
				picture = "junichiro_koizumi.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { 
					ruling_party = 6 
				} 
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Junichiro Koizumi"
				picture = "junichiro_koizumi.dds"
				ideology = Conservative
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
				}
			}
		}
		
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.15 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_country_flag = JAP_KOIZUMI_HISTRICAL_APPEARANCE

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

#Koizumi or Abe
country_event = {
	id = JAP_historical.20060926
	title = JAP_historical.20060926.t
	desc = JAP_historical.20060926.d
	#TODO:picture 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_country_leader = { name = "Junichiro Koizumi" }	
			has_country_flag = JAP_KOIZUMI_HISTRICAL_APPEARANCE
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = JAP_historical.20060926.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: JAP_historical.20060926.oA executed"

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = JAP_historical.20060926.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: JAP_historical.20060926.oB executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { 
					ruling_party = 0 
				} 
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Shinzo Abe"
				picture = "Shinzo_Abe.dds"
				ideology = Western_Autocracy
				traits = { 
					western_conservatism 
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { 
					ruling_party = 1 
				} 
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Shinzo Abe"

country_event = {
	id = JAP_historical.20070926
	title = JAP_historical.20070926.t
	desc = JAP_historical.20070926.d
	#TODO:picture 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_country_leader = { name = "Shinzo Abe" }	
			has_country_flag = JAP_ABE_FIRST_HISTRICAL_APPEARANCE
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = JAP_historical.20070926.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: JAP_historical.20070926.oA executed"

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = JAP_historical.20070926.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: JAP_historical.20070926.oB executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { 
					ruling_party = 0 
				} 
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yasuo Fukuda" 
				picture = "yasuo_fukuda.dds" 
				ideology = Western_Autocracy
				traits = {
					western_conservatism 
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { 
					ruling_party = 1 
				} 
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yasuo Fukuda" 
				picture = "yasuo_fukuda.dds" 
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = { 
					western_conservatism 
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { 
					ruling_party = 6 
				} 
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yasuo Fukuda" 
				picture = "yasuo_fukuda.dds" 
				ideology = Conservative
				traits = { 
					western_conservatism 
				}
			}
		}
		
		set_country_flag = JAP_FUKUDA_HISTRICAL_APPEARANCE

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#3.11
country_event = {
	id = JAP_historical.20110311
	title = JAP_historical.20110311.t
	desc = JAP_historical.20110311.d
	#picture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		controls_state = 616
		controls_state = 615
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { JAP_once_millennium_disaster_stability_factor = -0.15 }
		set_variable = { JAP_once_millennium_disaster_political_power_factor = -0.20 }
		set_variable = { JAP_once_millennium_disaster_consumer_goods_factor = 0.20 }
		set_variable = { JAP_once_millennium_disaster_energy_gain_multiplier = -0.20 }
		616 = {
			set_variable = { JAP_scars_earthquake_and_tsunami_state_production_speed_buildings_factor = -0.50 }
		 	set_variable = { JAP_scars_earthquake_and_tsunami_state_resources_factor = -0.30 }
			set_variable = { JAP_scars_earthquake_and_tsunami_state_productivity_growth_modifier = -0.30 }
		}
		615 = {
			set_variable = { JAP_scars_earthquake_state_production_speed_buildings_factor = -0.20 }
		 	set_variable = { JAP_scars_earthquake_state_resources_factor = -0.15 }
		 	set_variable = { JAP_scars_earthquake_state_productivity_growth_modifier = -0.10 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = JAP_historical.20110311.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: JAP_historical.20110311.a executed"
		616 = {
			remove_building = { type = infrastructure level = 4 }
			remove_building = { type = internet_station level = 2 }
			remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 4 }
			remove_building = { type = dockyard level = 1 }
			remove_building = { type = agriculture_district level = 1 }
			damage_building = { type = arms_factory damage = 5.0 }
			damage_building = { type = offices damage = 5.0 }
			add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = JAP_scars_earthquake_and_tsunami
			}
		}
		newline = yes
		615 = {
			remove_building = { type = infrastructure level = 2 }
			remove_building = { type = internet_station level = 1 }
			remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 3 }
			damage_building = { type = arms_factory damage = 2.0 }
			damage_building = { type = dockyard damage = 2.0 }
			damage_building = { type = agriculture_district damage = 2.0 }
			damage_building = { type = offices damage = 2.0 }
			add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = JAP_scars_earthquake
			}
		}
		newline = yes
		decrease_economic_growth = yes
		newline = yes
		add_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = JAP_once_millennium_disaster
		}
		newline = yes
		add_manpower = -18420
		newline = yes
		every_country = { news_event = JAP_news.02 }
		newline = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_great_east_japan_earthquake_tree_tt
		set_country_flag = JAP_great_east_japan_earthquake_flag
		

		ai_chance = {
			 base = 1
		}
	}
}

#North Korea Prepares For War
country_event = {
	id = Japan.200004000
	title = Japan.200004000.t
	desc = Japan.200004000.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = JAP
		NKO = {
			focus_progress = {
				focus = NKO_remilitarize_the_DMZ
				progress > 0.2
			}
		}
		#TODO: add the flag for choosing to help assist NKO, otherwise we don't care
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 5 }

	#Encourage NKO to de-escalate
	option = {
		name = Japan.200004000.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.200004000.oA"
		add_political_power = -150
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 3 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 5 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		#TODO: event for NKO: "Japan Responds to Aggression"
	}

	#Withdraw all support
	option = {
		name = Japan.200004000.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.200004000.oB"
		add_war_support = 0.05
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 2 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 2 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		#TODO: event for NKO: "Japan Rescinds Aid"
		#TODO: event for KOR: "Japan Rescinds Aid To North Korea"
		#TODO: store party in charge that supported aid to Korea, and reduce support for them
	}

	#Secret Talks Against KOR (only if KOR is being aggressive)
}

#American Financial Crisis: Hits Japan (JAP)
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100015000
	title = Japan.100015000.t
	desc = Japan.100015000.d
	picture = WIP #TODO: gfx

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#We need to overcome this together
	option = {
		name = Japan.100015000.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100015000.oA"
		decrease_two_level_economic_growth = yes
		add_stability = -0.05
		#TODO: bonus to liberals popularity
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 15 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 10 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		#TODO: custom tooltip: will require us to spend money to escape the recession
		country_event = { id = Japan.100015020 days = 5 } #american financial crisis: hands across the pacific
	}

	#This is the fault of reckless globalization!
	option = {
		name = Japan.100015000.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100015000.oB"
		decrease_two_level_economic_growth = yes
		remove_ideas = JAP_ftaap_member
		USA = {
			remove_ideas = JAP_ftaap_member
		}
		#TODO: big penalty to liberals popularity
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = JAP_ftaap_member
			}
			country_event = { id = Japan.100015010 random_days = 5 } #american financial crisis: dissolution of the FTAAP
		}
		country_event = { id = Japan.100015010 days = 7 } #american financial crisis: the shattering
	}
}

#American Financial Crisis: The Shattering
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100015010
	title = Japan.100015010.t
	desc = Japan.100015010.d
	desc = {
		text = Japan.100015010.d.a #USA left the FTAAP on bad terms
		trigger = {
			USA = {
				has_country_flag = JAP_RECESSION_USA_REJECTED_SOVEREIGNTY
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = Japan.100015010.d.b #JAP terminated the FTAAP in response to recession aftershocks
	}
	picture = WIP #TODO: gfx

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Free Trade with Asians Only
	option = {
		name = Japan.100015010.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100015010.oA"
		#TODO: EAEC invitation focuses should take less time to finish, higher penalty to include australia/nz
		add_ideas = JAP_seap_member
		if = {
			limit = {
				USA = {
					has_country_flag = JAP_RECESSION_USA_REJECTED_SOVEREIGNTY
				}
			}
			every_other_country = { #FTAAP exists but is collapsing with USA's exit
				limit = {
					has_idea = JAP_ftaap_member
				}
				country_event = { id = Japan.100015011 random_days = 2 random_hours = 12 } #american financial crisis: revive FTAAP as SEAP
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_other_country = { #invite countries that used to be in FTAAP and still want to be back
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = JAP_FTAAP_FORMER_MEMBER
				}
				country_event = { id = Japan.100015011 random_days = 2 random_hours = 12 } #american financial crisis: revive FTAAP as SEAP
			}
		}
	}

	#End Free Trade entirely!
	option = {
		name = Japan.100015010.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100015010.oB"
		#TODO: EPA focuses should take less time to finish
		#TODO: big bonus to nationalist
	}
}

#Pyongyang Visit: Request to JAP
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100010006
	title = Japan.100010006.t
	desc = {
		text = Japan.100010006.d.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = JAP_NKO_CONF_ABDUCTIONS_DEMAND
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = Japan.100010006.d.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = JAP_NKO_CONF_NUCLEAR_DEMAND
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = Japan.100010006.d.c
	}
	picture = WIP #TODO: gfx

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = NKO
		NKO = {
			has_war = no
		}
	}

	#Request Food Aid
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				NKO = { has_country_flag = JAP_NKO_CONF_ABDUCTIONS_DEMAND }
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		name = Japan.100010006.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100010006.oA"
		JAP = {
			set_country_flag = JAP_NKO_CONF_FOOD_DEMAND
			country_event = { id = Japan.100010007 days = 1 } # JAP's turn to hear demands
		}
		#TODO: custom tooltip to show AI JAP will always accept this
	}

	#Request Industrial Assistance
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				NKO = { has_country_flag = JAP_NKO_CONF_NUCLEAR_DEMAND }
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		name = Japan.100010006.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100010006.oB"
		JAP = {
			set_country_flag = JAP_NKO_CONF_INDUSTRIAL_DEMAND
			country_event = { id = Japan.100010007 days = 1 } # JAP's turn to hear demands
		}
		#TODO: custom tooltip if relations not good enough to guarantee success
	}

	#Request Recognition
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				NKO = { has_country_flag = JAP_NKO_CONF_NO_DEMAND }
				factor = 3
			}
			#TODO: more likely if KOR has taken sunshine policy OR if JAP requested rapprochement only
		}
		name = Japan.100010006.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100010006.oC"
		JAP = {
			set_country_flag = JAP_NKO_CONF_LEGITIMACY_DEMAND
			if = {
				limit = {
					KOR = { has_completed_focus = KOR_sunshine_policy }
				}
				country_event = { id = Japan.100010008 days = 1 } # JAP's turn to hear demands (sunshine)
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = Japan.100010009 days = 1 } # JAP's turn to hear demands (exclude KOR)
			}
		}
		#TODO: custom tooltip if relations not good enough to guarantee success
	}

	#Reject!
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		name = Japan.100010006.oD
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100010006.oD"
		NKO = {
			set_country_flag = JAP_NKO_CONF_FAILURE
		}
		JAP = {
			set_country_flag = JAP_NKO_CONF_FAILURE
			country_event = { id = Japan.100010010 days = 1 } # Visit is a Failure
		}
	}
}

#Japan's offer of the oil interests in Diaoyutai
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1770802
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1770802.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1770802.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_SMALL } }
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = { is_capital = yes }
					add_resource = { type = oil amount = 2 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_MIDDLE } }
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = { is_capital = yes }
					add_resource = { type = oil amount = 4 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_LARGE } }
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = { is_capital = yes }
					add_resource = { type = oil amount = 8 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Accept their offer
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1770802.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1770802.oA"
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1770803 days = 1 } }
	}

	#Refuse and keep our claim
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_SMALL }
				add = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_MIDDLE }
				add = 25
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1770802.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1770802.oB"
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1770805 days = 1 } }
	}
}

			random_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_capital = yes }
				add_resource = { type = oil amount = 4 }
			}
			add_political_power = 40
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_LARGE } }
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_capital = yes }
				add_resource = { type = oil amount = 8 }
			}
			add_political_power = 80
		}
		939 = {
			remove_core_of = ROOT
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
	}
}

#First Choice (2000)
country_event = {
	id = Japan_Demographic.100000101
	title = Japan_Demographic.100000101.t
	desc = Japan_Demographic.100000101.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Support for families
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100000101.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100000101.oA"
		set_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_APPEALED_CONSERVATIVES
		add_political_power = 50
		increase_social_spending = yes
		block_social_decrease = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			steal_popularity_from_conservatives = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	#Talk up workers' rights
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100000101.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100000101.oB"
		set_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_APPEALED_PROGRESSIVES
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.02
		if = {
			limit = { has_economically_liberal_government = yes }
			steal_popularity_from_progressives = yes
			set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -5 }
			change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
			change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes
			change_international_bankers_opinion = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#Conservatives Demand More
country_event = {
	id = Japan_Demographic.100000102
	title = Japan_Demographic.100000102.t
	desc = Japan_Demographic.100000102.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_small_shop

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		has_economically_liberal_government = yes
		has_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_APPEALED_CONSERVATIVES
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = fast_growth
				has_idea = economic_boom
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 365
		modifier = {
			has_stability < 0.5
			factor = 0.2
		}
		modifier = { # if economy stays healthy, stay off player's back
			has_idea = fast_growth
			factor = 3
		}
		modifier = { # if economy stays healthy, stay off player's back
			has_idea = economic_boom
			factor = 5
		}
	}

	#Accept
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100000102.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100000102.oA"
		set_temp_variable = { corp_change = -3 }
		modify_corporate_tax_rate_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes
		change_international_bankers_opinion = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	#Stuff it!
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100000102.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100000102.oB"
		add_political_power = -150
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -10 }
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes
		change_international_bankers_opinion = yes
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.01 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#Progressives Demand More
country_event = {
	id = Japan_Demographic.100000103
	title = Japan_Demographic.100000103.t
	desc = Japan_Demographic.100000103.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_labor_protest

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		has_economically_liberal_government = yes
		has_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_APPEALED_PROGRESSIVES
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = JAP_protect_worker_rights
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 365
		modifier = {
			has_stability < 0.5
			factor = 0.6
		}
	}

	#No way!
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100000103.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100000103.oA"
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.10 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.10 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_REFUSED_PROGRESSIVES

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	#Accept union interests
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100000103.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100000103.oB"
		add_political_power = -300
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = industrial_conglomerates
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = industrial_conglomerates
				add_idea = labour_unions
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 7 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 15 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 21 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#First Depopulation Checkup Gate (2002)
#This is more gentle in consequences than the main sequence checkups
country_event = {
	id = Japan_Demographic.100000320
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100000320.oA"
		if = { #You blew it!!
			limit = {
				check_variable = { jap_demographics_depopulation_reform < 1 }
			}
			JAP = { country_event = Japan_Demographic.100000321 }
		} else_if = { #Problems ahead!
			limit = {
				check_variable = { jap_demographics_depopulation_reform < 2 }
			}
			JAP = { country_event = Japan_Demographic.100000322 }
		} else = { #Doing great!
			JAP = { country_event = Japan_Demographic.100000323 }
		}
	}
}

#First Depopulation Checkup, Big Problems!
country_event = {
	id = Japan_Demographic.100000321
	title = Japan_Demographic.100000321.t
	desc = Japan_Demographic.100000321.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_hikikomori

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#These things take time...
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100000321.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100000321.oA"
		add_political_power = -300
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		JAP_demographics_depopulation_increase_1 = yes
		activate_mission = JAP_demographic_main_reminder

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	#Make some immediate changes
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100000321.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100000321.oB"
		add_political_power = -100
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -30 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		increase_social_spending = yes
		block_social_decrease = yes
		JAP_demographics_depopulation_increase_1 = yes
		activate_mission = JAP_demographic_main_reminder

		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
		}
	}

	#Opposition offers solutions!
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100000321.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100000321.oC"
		add_political_power = -100
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.10 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.10 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		JAP_demographics_depopulation_increase_1 = yes
		activate_mission = JAP_demographic_main_reminder

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}

#First Depopulation Checkup, No Problems
country_event = {
	id = Japan_Demographic.100000323
	title = Japan_Demographic.100000323.t
	desc = Japan_Demographic.100000323.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_prosperous_asakusa

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Great!
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100000323.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100000323.oA"
		add_political_power = 50
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		activate_mission = JAP_demographic_main_reminder

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}

	#Extend our program!
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100000323.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100000323.oB"
		increase_social_spending = yes
		set_temp_variable = { corp_change = 2 }
		modify_corporate_tax_rate_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { pop_change = 2 }
		modify_population_tax_rate_effect = yes
		if = { #only if eco conservative
			limit = { has_economically_liberal_government = yes }
			steal_popularity_from_progressives = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		activate_mission = JAP_demographic_main_reminder

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}

	#Amend the budget
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100000323.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100000323.oC"
		add_political_power = 100
		set_temp_variable = { corp_change = -3 }
		modify_corporate_tax_rate_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 50 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		if = { #only if not already conservative
			limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			steal_popularity_from_conservatives = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		activate_mission = JAP_demographic_main_reminder

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#Replace Industrial Conglomerates with Labor Union?
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100001001
	title = Japan.100001001.t
	desc = Japan.100001001.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_labor_protest

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		has_idea = industrial_conglomerates
		NOT = {
			has_idea = labour_unions
		}
	}

	#Better not
	option = {
		name = Japan.100001001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100001001.oA"
		add_political_power = 100

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	#Accept union interests
	option = {
		name = Japan.100001001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100001001.oB"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = industrial_conglomerates
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = industrial_conglomerates
				add_idea = labour_unions
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -200
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 10 }
		change_labour_unions_opinion = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 7 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 15 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 21 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}


# Samurai Bonds Chain
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100002000
	title = Japan.100002000.t
	desc = Japan.100002000.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_yen

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #accept deal
		name = Japan.100002000.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100002000.oA executed"
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 30 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		FROM = {
			country_event = Japan.100002001
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 0.5 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = FROM.id }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = ROOT.id }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = economic_mission
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = economic_mission
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #refuse deal
		name = Japan.100002000.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100002000.oB executed"
		FROM = {
			country_event = Japan.100002002
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = Japan.100004010.t
	desc = Japan.100004010.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_anchor_generic

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Accept deal
	option = {
		name = Japan.100004010.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100004010.oA executed"
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = Japan.100004010.t
			bonus = 1
			uses = 1
			category = CAT_internet_tech
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 0.5 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = FROM.id }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = ROOT.id }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					OR = { #only care to get a receipt from global if a major power or larger accepts
						has_idea = superpower
						has_idea = great_power
						has_idea = large_power
					}
					OR = { #if SEA, we want to know and potentially offer investments
						is_asean_nation = yes
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				country_event = Japan.100004011
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Refuse deal
	option = {
		name = Japan.100004010.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100004010.oB executed"
		add_political_power = 25

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Contribution to IHPCO
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100004141
	title = Japan.100004141.t
	desc = Japan.100004141.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_anchor_generic

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Accept
	option = {
		name = Japan.100004141.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100004141.oA executed"
		add_to_variable = {
			var = JAP.jap_ihcpo_funding_amt
			value = 1
		}
		FROM = { country_event = Japan.100004142 }
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -10 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		add_to_array = { FROM.jap_ihpco_members = ROOT.id }

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Refuse
	option = {
		name = Japan.100004141.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100004141.oB executed"
		add_political_power = 25
		FROM = { country_event = Japan.100004143 }

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# More Funding
	option = {
		name = Japan.100004141.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100004141.oC executed"
		add_to_variable = {
			var = JAP.jap_ihcpo_funding_amt
			value = 2
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -30 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		add_to_array = { FROM.jap_ihpco_members = ROOT.id }
		FROM = { country_event = Japan.100004142 }

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 30
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Supercomputing Results Gate
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100004144
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100004144.oA"
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { jap_ihcpo_funding_amt < 5 }
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = JAP.jap_ihpco_members
				country_event = { id = Japan.100004145 } # Supercomputing Bad Outcome
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { jap_ihcpo_funding_amt < 8 }
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = JAP.jap_ihpco_members
				country_event = { id = Japan.100004146 } # Supercomputing Good Outcome
			}
		} else = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = JAP.jap_ihpco_members
				country_event = { id = Japan.100004147 } # Supercomputing Amazing Outcome
			}
		}
	}
}

	# LDP Dominance

		add_stability = 0.03
		add_political_power = 50
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
	# Emerging LDP
	option = {
		name = Japan.100004200.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100004200.oB executed"
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = minor_improve_trade }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = minor_improve_trade }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}

		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
	# Sunrise/JIP/JRP
	option = {

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100004200.oE executed"
		add_stability = 0.03

######Japan-Any country Petrochemical Investments
country_event = {
	id = japan_foreign_policy.288
	title = japan_foreign_policy.288.t
	desc = japan_foreign_policy.288.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_CAN_keystone_pipeline_building
	option = {
		name = japan_foreign_policy.288.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: japan_foreign_policy.288.a executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value > 10
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = { country_event = japan_foreign_policy.29 }
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 6 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = JAP }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = ROOT }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		random_owned_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = fossil_powerplant
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_resource = {
				type = oil
				amount = 2
			}
		}
		newline = yes
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -4.00 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = japan_foreign_policy.288.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: japan_foreign_policy.288.b executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value < 10
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = { country_event = japan_foreign_policy.30 }
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = japan_foreign_policy.29
	title = japan_foreign_policy.29.t
	desc = japan_foreign_policy.29.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_CAN_keystone_pipeline_building
	option = {
		name = japan_foreign_policy.29.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: japan_foreign_policy.29.a executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -4.00 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		random_owned_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = fossil_powerplant
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_resource = {
				type = oil
				amount = 2
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 6 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_index = JAP }
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = FROM }
				change_influence_percentage = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = japan_foreign_policy.31
	title = japan_foreign_policy.31.t
	desc = japan_foreign_policy.31.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_SOV_generic
	option = {
		name = japan_foreign_policy.31.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: japan_foreign_policy.31.a executed"
		add_stability = 0.1
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.1 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		remove_state_claim = 690
		remove_state_core = 690
		SOV = { country_event = { id = japan_foreign_policy.32 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				has_opinion = {
					target = SOV
					value > 25
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = japan_foreign_policy.31.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: japan_foreign_policy.31.b executed"
		SOV = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.91760202 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				has_opinion = {
					target = SOV
					value < 10
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = japan_foreign_policy.31.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: japan_foreign_policy.31.c executed"
		add_political_power = -100
		SOV = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.91760242 days = 1 } }
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 1 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				has_opinion = {
					target = SOV
					value < 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = JAP_territorial.01
	title = JAP_territorial.01.t
	desc = JAP_territorial.01.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = JAP_territorial.01.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: JAP_territorial.01.oA executed"
		SOV = { country_event = JAP_territorial.02 }
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

#[JAP.GetName] Requests Northern Territories Negotiations
country_event = {
	id = JAP_territorial.02
	title = JAP_territorial.02.t
	desc = JAP_territorial.02.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = JAP_territorial.02.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: JAP_territorial.01.oA executed"
		1168 = { 
			transfer_state_to = JAP
		}
		SOV = {
			 remove_state_core = 1168 
			 remove_opinion_modifier = {
				target = JAP
				modifier = minor_border_dispute
			}
		}
		JAP = { 
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = minor_border_dispute
			}
			country_event = {
				id = JAP_territorial.03
				days = 5
			} 
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value > 25
				}
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value < 50
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value > 49
				}
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value < 75
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 2.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value > 74
				}
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value < 100
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 3.0
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value > 99
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				sender_influence_higher_10 = yes
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 2.5
				sender_influence_higher_15 = yes
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 3.0
				sender_influence_higher_25 = yes
			}
		}
		#opinion60,influence20 = 1.0*2.0*2.0*2.5 = 10.0 10.0/10.0+10 = 0.5
		#opinion100,infuluence30 = 1.0*3.0*2.0*2.5*3.0 = 45.0 45.0/45.0+10 = 0.818
	}

	option = {
		name = JAP_territorial.02.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: JAP_territorial.01.oB executed"

#[JAP.GetName] Proposes Territorial Negotiations
country_event = {
	id = JAP_territorial.06
	title = JAP_territorial.06.t
	desc = JAP_territorial.06.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = JAP_territorial.06.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: JAP_territorial.06.oA executed"
		939 = {
			remove_claim_by = CHI
		}
		CHI = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				target = JAP
				modifier = minor_border_dispute
			}
		}
		JAP = { 
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				target = CHI
				modifier = minor_border_dispute
			}
			country_event = {
				id = JAP_territorial.07
				days = 5
			}  
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value > 25
				}
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value < 50
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value > 49
				}
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value < 75
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 2.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value > 74
				}
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value < 100
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 3.0
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value > 99
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				sender_influence_higher_10 = yes
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 2.5
				sender_influence_higher_15 = yes
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 3.0
				sender_influence_higher_25 = yes
			}
		}
		#opinion60,influence20 = 1.0*2.0*2.0*2.5 = 10.0 10.0/10.0+10 = 0.5
		#opinion100,infuluence30 = 1.0*3.0*2.0*2.5*3.0 = 45.0 45.0/45.0+10 = 0.818
	}

	option = {
		name = JAP_territorial.06.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: JAP_territorial.06.oB executed"
		add_political_power = -50
		JAP = { 
			country_event = {
				id = JAP_territorial.08
				days = 5
			}  
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
    id = JAP_diplomacy.10
    hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: JAP_diplomacy.10 executed"

		JAP = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = JAP_kor_accept_intellectual_platform
					has_country_flag = JAP_chi_accept_intellectual_platform
				}
				country_event = {
					id = JAP_diplomacy.08
					days = 3
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = JAP_diplomacy.09
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
    id = JAP_diplomacy.31
    title = JAP_diplomacy.31.t
    desc  = JAP_diplomacy.31.d

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = JAP_diplomacy.31.a
        log  = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: JAP_diplomacy.31.a executed"
		custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_change_landforce_tt
		set_temp_variable = {
			JAP_max_planning_landforces_change = 0.10
		}
		update_JAP_max_planning_landforces_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			JAP_recon_factor_landforces_change = 0.15
		}
		update_JAP_recon_factor_landforces_effect = yes
		newline = yes
        if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = jap_kaguya_satellite_invest }
			custom_effect_tooltip = jap_kaguya_satellite_invest_tt
            add_tech_bonus = {
                bonus    = 0.75
                uses     = 2
                category = CAT_satellite
            }
        }
		if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = jap_kaguya_rocketry_invest }
			custom_effect_tooltip = jap_kaguya_rocketry_invest_tt
            add_tech_bonus = {
                bonus    = 0.5
                uses     = 2
                category = CAT_missile
            }
			newline = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_change_airforce_tt
			set_temp_variable = {
				JAP_strategic_bomb_visibility_airforce_change = 0.15
			}
			update_JAP_strategic_bomb_visibility_airforce_effect = yes
        }
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 2 }
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_country_flag = JAP_moon_base_completed
    }
}

			}
		}
